      <h3 class="trust-title">
       Blasting News adheres to The Trust Project - News with Integrity quality standards.
      </h3>
     </div>
     <div class="trust-text">
      We follow the transparency standards developed by the
      <a href="https://thetrustproject.org/" target='\"_blank\"'>
       'Trust Project - News with Integrity'
      </a>
      , promoted by the University of Santa Clara, which establishes principles to keep journalism accurate and transparent. Blasting News is not a member of the programme, but has requested to be part of it; The Trust Project has not conducted an audit yet.
     </div>
    </div>

   <div class="about-inner">
    <div class="single-about open">
     <h3 class="about-title">
      Mission and values
     </h3>
     <div class="about-text">
      <p>
       Blasting News is an innovative global publisher whose main objective is to offer independent and accurate journalism. We tell our news from a multiplicity of angles, without taking sides. Different from all other publishers who express their own agendas and prefer one point of view over another, at Blasting News the only side we take is yours: we offer you the story from every angle, even if we dont agree with all of them, so that you can build informed opinions.
      </p>
      <span>
       For us, every voice counts: this is the reason why we are open to receive submissions from any collaborator and freelancer. However, openness demands responsibility. To create a safe environment, all our news articles are submitted to a rigorous curation and fact-checking process using industry best practices: every piece of content is screened firstly by a Reviewer, than by our internal newsroom in London.
       <ul class="about-text-link-inline">
        <li>
         <a href="https://www.blastingnews.com/about-us/" target="_blank">
          More about us
         </a>
        </li>
       </ul>
      </span>
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="single-about open" id="single-about-channel">
     <h3 class="about-title">
      Follow your passions (the Channels)
     </h3>
     <div class="about-text">
      <span>
       Channels are communities of engaged users around specific vertical topics. You can keep up with all the latest news about the topics you love simply following the Channels around the things that interest you the most. Blasting News' Channels are a unique blend of verified and professionally curated news, written by our contributors and verified by our Reviewers, but also from official social media accounts and a lot of other leading publisher feeds. You wont find a coverage like this anywhere else.
      </span>
     </div>

      Staff &amp; Corporate
     </h3>
     <div class="about-text">

       Blasting News relies on 2,000 contributors, with no limitation of race, class, age, gender and geography. Furthermore, Blasting News seeks diverse voices in its management staff. We employee professionals from more than 7 different nationalities in our offices in London (headquarters), Milan, New York and Rome. We are an independent, private company funded by a number of private shareholders and family offices. As a result, business decisions, but not editorial decisions, take shareholder value in mind.

    var cookieBanner$ = document.getElementById("cookie-content");

        if(window._acC == null || window._tcs == null) {
      var _waitForTCS = function(event) {
        if (event.origin.indexOf('blastingnews.com') == -1) return;
        try {
          var data = JSON.parse(event.data || null);
          if(data.type === 'tcString') {
            window.__tcs = data.string;
            if(window.__acC !== null) {
              _checkConsents();
              window.removeEventListener('message', _waitForTCS);
            }
          } else if(data.type === 'googAC') {
            window.__acC = data.string;
            if(window.__tcs !== null) {
              _checkConsents();
              window.removeEventListener('message', _waitForTCS);
            }
          } 
        } catch {          
        }
      }
      window.addEventListener('message', _waitForTCS);
    }
